msg:I came to Yangzhou with my 10-month-old baby. At first, I chose this hotel because it was close to the Slender West Lake, but after moving in, I was moved by the hotel's service and environment.
Location: The hotel is in an excellent location, right next to the South Gate of the Slender West Lake. If you choose to take a boat from the South Gate to the Twenty-Four Bridges and walk back like me, the pier is just opposite the hotel, which is simply as close as it can be.
Environment: Clean and sanitary. There are many camping tents at the door of the hotel. It is not too comfortable to blow the wind at the door after breakfast or at night.
Facilities: Restaurants, gyms, children's playgrounds, etc. are complete. My baby is 10 months old and plays in the children's playground for one or two hours almost every day. Although it is not big, it is enough for her to play. Umbrellas and strollers are also provided in the lobby. The fruit drinks at the door are delicious. Basically, I have to drink a cup every time I pass by.
Catering: Because it is in the Hongqiaofang Resort, there are many food, convenience stores, and cafes around, which is very convenient. The hotel breakfast is quite satisfactory, focusing on convenience and hygiene. White porridge and boiled eggs in white water basically solve my baby's daily supplementary food.
Service: This is really important to write about. From the lobby to the room service, it can be said that it is meticulous. When you go out or come back, the staff will help you open the door and take things. It is really helpful for me to bring my children. Let‚Äôs talk about the room butler. My butler is called Xiaoying and Xiaoliang. On the first day of check-in, the butler recommended me the surrounding food and attractions. When it rained halfway, he would ask me where I was and asked to drive to pick us up. Because of the constant accidents with children, my child got sick on the second day of check-in. The butler was still concerned until the next day and took the child to the hospital. It was really heartwarming ‚ù§Ô∏è. Because of this, our itinerary changed, and we asked to extend our stay and immediately assisted in the arrangement. In short, it really added a lot of points to our trip to Yangzhou.

If you come to Yangzhou to play, it is highly recommended (#^.^#)üëçüèª
